<h1 _ngcontent-isj-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Search"> Search </h1>

<div _ngcontent-isj-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>搜索框组件，适用于浏览器的搜索内容输入框等应用场景。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 8开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>      <p>该组件仅支持单文本样式，若需实现富文本样式，建议使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-richeditor">RichEditor</a>组件。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>无</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 429px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Search(options?: SearchOptions)</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数:</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#searchoptions18对象说明">SearchOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">搜索框组件初始化选项</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1784px;">     <h2 id="searchoptions18对象说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">SearchOptions<sup>18+</sup>对象说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="searchoptions18对象说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Search初始化参数。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>为规范匿名对象的定义，API 18版本修改了此处的元素定义。其中，保留了历史匿名对象的起始版本信息，会出现外层元素@since版本号高于内层元素版本号的情况，但这不影响接口的使用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">value<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置当前显示的搜索文本内容。</p>          <p>从API version 10开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-two-way-sync" target="_blank">$$</a>双向绑定变量。</p>          <p>从API version 18开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-new-binding#系统组件参数双向绑定" target="_blank">!!</a>双向绑定变量。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <p>从API version 20开始，支持Resource类型。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">placeholder<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置无输入时的提示文本。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">icon<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置搜索图标路径，默认使用系统搜索图标。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>icon的数据源支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-image#示例25使用相对路径显示图片">使用相对路径显示图片</a>和网络图片。</p>          <p>- 支持的图片格式包括png、jpg、bmp、svg、gif、pixelmap和heif。</p>          <p>- 支持Base64字符串。格式data:image/[png|jpeg|bmp|webp|heif];base64,[base64 data], 其中[base64 data]为Base64字符串数据。</p>          <p>如果与属性searchIcon同时设置，则searchIcon优先。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">controller<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#searchcontroller">SearchController</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置Search组件控制器。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>外，还支持以下属性：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 810px;">     <h3 id="searchbutton" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">searchButton<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="searchbutton" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>searchButton(value: ResourceStr, option?: SearchButtonOptions)</p>     <p>设置搜索框末尾搜索按钮。</p>     <p>点击搜索按钮，同时触发onSubmit与onClick回调。</p>     <p>Wearable设备上默认字体大小为18fp。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td <p>}</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="placeholdercolor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">placeholderColor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="textfont" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textFont<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textfont" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textFont(value?: Font)</p>     <p>设置搜索框内输入文本样式，包括字体大小、字体粗细、字体族、字体风格。</p>     <p>Wearable设备上默认字体大小为18fp。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#font">Font</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">搜索框内输入文本样式。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 633px;">     <h3 id="textalign9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textAlign<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textalign9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textAlign(value: TextAlign)</p>     <p>设置文本在搜索框中的对齐方式。目前支持的对齐方式有：TextAlign.Start、TextAlign.Center、TextAlign.End。TextAlign.JUSTIFY的对齐方式按照TextAlign.Start处理。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textalign">TextAlign</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本在搜索框中的对齐方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextAlign.Start</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>textAlign只能调整文本整体的布局，不影响字符的显示顺序。若需要调整字符的显示顺序，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-internationalization#镜像状态字符对齐" target="_blank">镜像状态字符对齐</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="copyoption9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">copyOption<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="copyoption9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>copyOption(value: CopyOptions)</p>     <p>设置输入的文本是否可复制。设置CopyOptions.None时，当前Search中的文字无法被复制、剪切、翻译、分享、搜索和帮写，支持粘贴和全选。</p>     <p>设置CopyOptions.None时，不允许拖拽。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.12.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#copyoptions9">CopyOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>输入的文本是否可复制。</p>          <p>默认值：CopyOptions.LocalDevice，支持设备内复制。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否不弹出系统文本选择菜单。</p>          <p>设置为true时，单击输入框光标、长按输入框、双击输入框、三击输入框或者右键输入框，不弹出系统文本选择菜单。</p>          <p>设置为false时，弹出系统文本选择菜单。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 942px;">     <h3 id="customkeyboard10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">customKeyboard<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="customkeyboard10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>customKeyboard(value: CustomBuilder, options?: KeyboardOptions)</p>     <p>设置自定义键盘。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，输入框激活后不会打开系统输入法，而是加载指定的自定义组件。</p>     <p>自定义键盘的高度可以通过自定义组件根节点的height属性设置，宽度不可设置，使用系统默认值。</p>     <p>自定义键盘采用覆盖原始界面的方式呈现，当没有开启避让模式或者输入框不需要避让的场景不会对应用原始界面产生压缩或者上提。</p>     <p>自定义键盘无法获取焦点，但是会拦截手势事件。</p>     <p>默认在输入控件失去焦点时，关闭自定义键盘，开发者也可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#stopediting10">stopEditing</a>方法控制键盘关闭。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，可以通过绑定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-key#onkeypreime12">onKeyPrelme</a>事件规避物理键盘的输入。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.14.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.14.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#custombuilder8">CustomBuilder</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">自定义键盘。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-richeditor#keyboardoptions12">KeyboardOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置自定义键盘是否支持避让功能。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 565px;">     <h3 id="type11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">type<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="type11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type(value: SearchType)</p>     <p>设置输入框类型。</p>     <p>不同的SearchType会拉起对应类型的键盘，同时限制输入。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead> class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>特殊字符字体高度远超出同行的其他字符高度时，文本框出现截断、遮挡、内容相对位置发生变化等不符合预期的显示异常，需要开发者调整组件高度、行高等属性，修改对应的页面布局。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 801px;">     <h3 id="decoration12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">decoration<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.24.7.1.5.1.2" class="content">       <p>当文字的下边缘轮廓与装饰线位置相交时，会触发下划线避让规则，下划线将在这些字符处避让文字。常见“gjyqp”等英文字符。</p>       <p>当文本装饰线的颜色设置为Color.Transparent时，装饰线颜色设置为跟随每行第一个字的字体颜色。当文本装饰线的颜色设置为透明色16进制对应值“#00FFFFFF”时，装饰线颜色设置为透明色。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="letterspacing12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">letterSpacing<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="letterspacing12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>letterSpacing(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本字符间距。设置该值为百分比时，按默认值显示。设置该值为0时，按默认值显示。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>当取值为负值时，文字会发生压缩，负值过小时会将组件内容区大小压缩为0，导致无内容显示。</p>     <p>对每个字符生效，包括行尾字符。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">            </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 853px;">     <h3 id="fontfeature12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontFeature<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fontfeature12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fontFeature(value: string)</p>     <p>设置文字特性效果，比如数字等宽的特性。</p>     <p>格式为：normal | &lt;feature-tag-value&gt;</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的格式为：&lt;string&gt; [ &lt;integer&gt; | on | off ]</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的个数可以有多个，中间用','隔开。</p>     <p>例如，使用等宽数字的输入格式为："ss01" on。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" <p>Font Feature当前支持的属性见 <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#fontfeature12">fontFeature属性列表</a>。</p>     <p>设置 Font Feature 属性，Font Feature 是 OpenType 字体的高级排版能力，如支持连字、数字等宽等特性，一般用在自定义字体中，其能力需要字体本身支持。</p>     <p>更多 Font Feature 能力介绍可参考 <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop" target="_blank">https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop</a> 和 <a href="https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/" id="inputfilter12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputFilter<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="inputfilter12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>inputFilter(value: ResourceStr, error?: Callback&lt; string &gt;)</p>     <p>通过正则表达式设置输入过滤器。匹配表达式的输入允许显示，不匹配的输入将被过滤。</p>     <p>单字符输入场景仅支持单字符匹配，多字符输入场景支持字符串匹配，例如粘贴。</p>     <p>设置inputFilter且输入的字符不为空字符，会导致设置输入框类型(即type接口)附带的文本过滤效果失效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">正则表达式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">error</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt; string &gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">正则匹配失败时，返回被过滤的内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="textindent12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textIndent<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon   </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a 637px;">     <h3 id="minfontsize12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">minFontSize<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="minfontsize12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最小显示字号。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#maxfontsize12">maxFontSize</a>以及布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>minFontSize小于或等于0时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#textfont">textFont</a>属性里面size的取值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#oncreatemenu12">onCreateMenu</a>的入参列表中不包含被屏蔽的菜单选项。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version id="enablepreviewtext12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enablePreviewText<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablepreviewtext12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enablePreviewText(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启输入预上屏。</p>     <p>预上屏内容定义为文字暂存态，目前不支持文字拦截功能。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否开启输入预上屏。</p>          <p>true表示开启输入预上屏，false表示不开启输入预上屏。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>“预上屏”描述的是一种文字暂存状态。需要在输入法中开启预上屏功能，在输入文本过程中，未确认输入候选词时，文本框中显示标记文本。例如，通过拼音输入中文时，未确定候选词之前，在输入框中显示拼音字母，该状态称为文字预上屏。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 842px;">     <h3 id="enablehapticfeedback13" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableHapticFeedback<sup>13+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablehapticfeedback13" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableHapticFeedback(isEnabled: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启触控反馈。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 13开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.2" class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>Search无文本内容时按钮置灰且不可点击。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p>          <p>true表示开启按钮置灰功能，false表示不开启。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="事件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">事件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" 501px;">     <h3 id="onsubmit" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onSubmit<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onsubmit" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onSubmit(callback: Callback&lt;string&gt;)</p>     <p>点击搜索图标、搜索按钮或者按下软键盘搜索按钮时触发该回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;string&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">搜索提交回调，其返回值为当前搜索框中输入的文本内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="onsubmit14" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onSubmit<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onsubmit14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onSubmit(callback: SearchSubmitCallback)</p>     <p>点击搜索图标、搜索按钮或者按下软键盘搜索按钮时触发该回调事件，提交事件时提供保持Search编辑状态的方法。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 14开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">点击搜索图标、搜索按钮或者按下软键盘搜索按钮时的回调事件。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="onchange" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onChange<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onchange" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span <p>在本回调中，若执行了光标操作，需要开发者在预上屏场景下依据previewText参数调整光标逻辑，以适应预上屏场景。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onWillAttachIME(callback: Callback&lt;IMEClient&gt;)</p>     <p>在搜索框将要绑定输入法前触发该回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 318px;">     <h3 id="stopediting10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">stopEditing<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon id="settextselection12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setTextSelection<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="settextselection12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setTextSelection(selectionStart: number, selectionEnd: number, options?: SelectionOptions): void;</p>     <p>组件在获焦状态下，调用该接口设置文本选择区域并高亮显示，且只有在selectionStart小于selectionEnd时，文字才会被选取并高亮显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">selectionStart</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本选择区域起始位置，文本框中文字的起始位置为0。</p>          <p>当selectionStart小于0时、按照0处理；当selectionStart大于文字最大长度时、按照文字最大长度处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">selectionEnd</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本选择区域结束位置。</p>          <p>当selectionEnd小于0时、按照0处理；当selectionEnd大于文字最大长度时、按照文字最大长度处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-text-style#selectionoptions12对象说明">SelectionOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>选中文字时的配置。</p>          <p>默认值：MenuPolicy.DEFAULT。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>如果selectionStart或selectionEnd被赋值为undefined时，当作0处理。</p>       <p>如果selectionMenuHidden被赋值为true或设备为2in1时，即使options被赋值为MenuPolicy.SHOW，调用setTextSelection也不弹出菜单。</p>       <p>如果选中的文本含有emoji表情时，表情的起始位置包含在设置的文本选中区域内就会被选中。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#onwilldelete12">onWillDelete</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#onwillchange15">onWillChange</a>接口展示了文本内容将要发生变化时的具体信息。</p>     <div _ngcontent-isj-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例10文本扩展自定义菜单" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>从API version 12开始，该示例通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-search#editmenuoptions12">editMenuOptions</a>接口实现了文本设置自定义菜单扩展项的文本内容、图标以及回调的功能，同时，可以在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#属性-1">onPrepareMenu</a>（从API version 20开始）回调中，进行菜单数据的设置。</p>     <div _ngcontent-isj-c106=""
